# INTRODUCTION

Four decades are over; the fifth is on. Research is being carried upon the births of persons born in the same locality with an interval of 10 minutes, 20 minutes and so on. I concentrated the study upon the horoscopes of the twin births. I collected data regarding the time of birth of the twins, the various results enjoyed by them and the time of such events. 

Whit carrying out such a research, I found that the general principles cruncated by our ancients and also those given out by the scholars of other countries cannot be strictly adhered to and applied to one and all: it is evident and clear, especially in twin hulls. In view the rule may not correct in the case of one but fails inaccurately in that of the other; the result is demonstrically opposite. With due respect to the learned authors and to the astrologists who strictly follow the principles, many consultants have complained to me that there is no coherence, no clarity, whereas confusion and contradiction do exist. They also have the same excuse, saying that plants show tendencies. A few twist the rules and astrology is thereby made useful only to the astrologist. Therefore, both the student of astrology and the astrologist themselves have to consciously confess that there is no simple, correct and convincing method which can be universally applied to one and all. This is a fact. 

By the grace of God, I evolved certain methods which are most convincing, very clear and pen-pointing to the time of event and explaining the nature of event to the entire satisfaction of the querist and the astrologer. It guides properly. So, this method, is the host and is very useful to the querists, as the prediction comes out correctly; also, it brings name and fame to the astrologer. 

Therefore, I am publishing the book on Horary System of Astrology after praying to God that the Truth which dawned in my mind, may be well explained, properly illustrated and exhaustively dealt with in a lucid manner. 

H.A-1 

# #

Let us first of all understand both the Hindu and the Western systems. 

# ASTROLOGY: HINDU AND WESTERN:

Some are under the wrong impression that the Westerners borrowed knowledge from the Hindus; some others say that the Hindus gained knowledge from the Chalcaam, Hebrews, Greeks and so on. Is the view correct? 

The segrs and the scholars in each country gazed at the stars, thousands of years ago, and they discovered the relation between the celestial phenomena and the terrestrial incidents. They established some methods to fit the provision of planets in the Zodiac and the consequent effect on the animale and inanimate objects on the earth. Each followed certain methods to protect the environment. If one has studied both the system, one will declare that another the Hindu hornweed from the Western, nor vice-versa. 

Suppose some students appeared for mathematically examining: copies of the question paper were distributed to them. All were busy answering them. The principal caught hold of a student called him as one who had been copying the answers written by another student, seated in front of him. He took this student and complained to the Headmaster that he had been copying in the examination hall. On enquiry, the student repeatedly said that he had not copied at all. The headmaster called for the assent of papers of both the students and compared them. He declared that the student had not copied at all and the computer was backed. 

The student, who was accused to have copied, had answered the questions 1, 3, 5 and 7 in the question paper. Wheras the other student had answered questions 2, 4, 6 and 8. Hence, the Headmaster who had gone through both the papers alone could know the truth. The superimponder who saw this student writing fast, and also, off and on, looking at the other student's table, had mistaken him, because both answered the same mathematics paper. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-04-29/990da3ce-db38-4a09-ad6f-9e97f5607c89/db19255016eb45ec55af2d8bdec25e89c5e6ecbbc940607b09750356f0ec1f8e.jpg)


Similarly, only when one studies both the Western and Hindu systems, we will confirm that the method followed by either is absolutely different from the other. 

1. Zediac: For both, the Zediac is the pathway of the planets. But for the Westerners, the commencement of the Zediac, i.e., Aries $0^{\circ}$ retrogadcs at the rate of roughly 50.2388475 seconds every year, whereas for the Hadius, for astrological purposes the Zediac commences always at a fixed point which is about $180^{\circ}$ from the Star Spica-Chubirai. The Zediac of the Wiaterners is called Sayana Zediac whereas that of the Hadius is called Nirayana Zediac. Therefore, as years pass on, in about 460 years, it will be found that the Sepr Aries-Meba called by the Hadius will actually circumcate with Taurun-Rahaba by the Wiatern. The purum of the Zediac called by the Hadius to Taurun-Rahaba will be called by Wiaterns as (Girmu-Mithnu and w on). 

3. Manleas: Watercarr have divided the Lodus into 12 equal parts and call them in Solar Mamions or signs. So also, Hindus have divided it into 12 equal parts and call each division as a Rani. But there is no difference in the commences- ment of the sign as explained above. Therefore, the area covered by the sign followed by the Watercarr and the Hindus is not the same. 

The Hindu have another method of dividing the Zodac. They have divided it upto 27 equal parts and call them as Lunar Mauwosa, Constellations. Asterram, Nakshihras or Sun. The Hindu give greater importance to this divinon They have found that planets transiting in the same sign but in different Nakshihras cause different effects. Just like each rasi (or sign) is said to be ruled by a planet, so also the Huidus declare that each star is governed by a particular planet (e.g.) Artes sign (Mesha) is ruled by Man (Sevval); Taurus Sign (Rababa) is governed by Venus (Satra); and so on. This is common to both the Western and the Hindu systems. But, after discovering Uranus and Neptune, the Westerners have allowed Aquarius (Kuma) to Uranus and Pisces (Meena) to Neptune. The 

Hindus did not include this allocation. As regards the Nakahatras, the first division commencing from Arios (Meha) $0^{\circ}$ is Arami ruled by Kctbu; the second is called Bharani governed by Venus; the third star is Karthikai ruled by Sun, the fourth Rohani, lord of which is Moon and so on. (It is given in a tabulated form in the Iu1 Krishnamurti Padhbhati.) 

3. Day: The Hindu consider that a day commences only from the moment of the Sunrise in that locality and that it extends till the next varuric in the same locality. The Sun may rise at 4-30 A.M or 5 A.M or 7-40 A.M If a child is born at 7-20 A.M. and the Sun rises only 7-40 A.M. In that locality on that day, then the child is said to have horn horn on the previous day. Suppose the Sun rises at 4-50 A.M and a child is born at 5-10 A.M. the Hindu consult that it is horn on the next day They take the lord of the next day for judgment and predict. This is very important when the Hindu act certain ayeepow day in undertale any project. As we follow civil date, date changs at 12 midnight Hui for Hindu Sunrise in Sunrise is a day, though, dae changs at 12 midnight. 

4. Heroscope: While creating a bony path and alkali predictive the Handoe attach much importance in the upper, homes and Navama position of the planets. But, the Watermen attach important, in the upper and houses. They have no "Navemoe" chart at all. 

5. The House, I.e. Bhava: Duffer widely between Eastern and Western system of calculation. Wacrnners calculate the hours from cusp to cusp, whereas the Hinder isle the cusp as the midpoint of the hour and call the Hour as Bhava. 

6. Prediction-Ududasa. Vimashobani, Ashtoiban, Kalachahra dwa, etc., are the various dasa advocated by the Hindu sages to product cals in one's life either to himself or w his relatives or others, with whom he $\mathcal{V}$ the has or has no transaction at all. The Woskrans have r.o data system at all. 

7. Progression: There is no clear and exhaustive method of "Progression" given by the Hindu seps though it is simply 

mentioned by only one sage. Westerners follow this method to predict events in one's life and have advanced much in Progression. 

8. Transit: Westerners take the position of Sun in the Sayana chart to offer transit results. The Sayana position of the transiting planets is referred to the position of Sun at birth. But the Hindus take the Nirayana position of the transiting planets and refer to the radical Narayana position of Moon in the horoscope. Further, the Hindus give the results according to the Sign occupied by the transiting planets and not the House (or Bhavas) transited by them; but the Westerner's take into consideration both the signs and the houses transited by the various planets and the exact longitudinal distance. 

9. Aspects: The Hindus are of opinion that all planets aspect the 7th house whereas Saturn has also special glance on the 3rd and 10th houses counted from the sign occupied by it. Jupiter aspects 5th and 9th houses from its position: Mar, aspects 4th and 8th houses, counted from the sign it occupies; other than the 7th. 

But the aspect followed by the Western are calculated correctly. They call that the longitude between one planet and another planet or one planet and the cusp of one house, if divisible by 22], the aspect is dharmonias, harmful and adverse. Also, they say "If the longitudinal distance among two planets, or between one planet and the cusp of another house, is divisible by 18" or $30^{\circ}$ (except 90' and 150') is considered to be harmonious, favourable and advantageous. They do not count sign to sign, as Hindu do; but they take the exact relative position. 

10. Parents: Westerners consider that the fourth house indicates father and the 10th house the mother. But the Hindus take the fourth house as the mother of the person and the 9th house as the father. 

11. Strength: Hindus estimate the strength of the planets by Shadbala, etc., after laborious work when as the method 

# #

adopted by the Westerners is very simple and they do not have any such calculation. 

12. Ashtraka varga: Is a method followed by the Hindus which is not known to the ancient astrologers of the West. This method is useless especially in Twin Birth Charts or to those born to different mothers within short interval. 

Thus, many instances can be given to show that the Westerners and Hindus follow their own system which are absolutely different. 

Why both the methods are considered to be uncomplete, and the Hindu System is confusing and contradicting needs no explanation. But one has to understand. 

(1) How to ascertain the favourable and the unfavourable disposition of planets. 

(2) What nature of results a plant indicates. 

(3) The exact time when they will be experienced 

(4) To predict the different results enjoyed by twins born in the same locality, but with an interval of few minutes even though the second (Lagna) is in the same sign, the position of planets in the Zodiac in the sign and in Nuvanna chart remains the same as well as the data and bhukti are more or less same. As per progression the aspect among the planets will also be similar in the horoscopes of people born within short interval. 

So, it would be a problem both for Hindus and Western men (1) to estimate the longevity of each, as in some cases, either of the two passes away early in infancy and the other lives along. (ii) one gets married, the other remains unmarried, (ui) one has a living character whereas the other is always after the opposite sex. (iv) one has children, the other has to adopt, (v) one enters Government service, the other takes up business. (vi) one is a lawyer, the other is a surgeon, and so on. The common aspects are the same mother, father, uncle, aunt, etc. But, 

the number of brothers and sisters will vary in those instances where one of the twins is a male and the other a female. 

Astrology can be declared a science, only when these differences can be explained properly. At least after knowing the results. It will be considered to be a perfect science, if it is made easy and the students having the ardent desire, understand it thoroughly, apply it properly and offer correct predictions. Herein came the need for research. 

By the Divine Grace, research was successful. Some truths are discovered. Later, after convincing my own conscience, from 1951 I began to teach my technique to many students (who are already karned). I am happy that God has given me wealth to tour throughout India and coach up hundreds of students every year. Everybody knows that I am the only astrologer doing this service. 

Also, a number of astrologers at Juan, Poona, Kirkce, Kyihapur, Sholapur and Ahmednagar waited me to deliver serice of kctun, daily, for 15 days and I did. 

A few cumc from Bombay to Delhi, stayed for months and attended lectures at Delhi. A few from Singapore, Kaspet, Bauswal and other places stayed in my residence and learnt Most of the disciples unlearnt what all they learnt prior to my lectures, thoroughly understood my technique Just like a number of parallel mirrors, reflect many images, and the images are seen to infinite distance, so also they make use of Krishnamurti Padhdbai, confirmed to be simple and supreme and spread this technique. They have declared that this is the best and correct method to foretell and satisfy the consultant as it enables one to offer precise predictions, even in the cases of twins born at an interval of only a few minutes. It is convincing, clear and very correct, that is what they say. There is no use for the word "Likely, Probably" etc. Tendency is used only by those people who cannot offer definite predictions. 

If this book is studied, one will say after studying once "Aham Na Panditlaka". A second reading will give him 

courage and confidence to say "Aham Cha Pandithaha". If a third reading is given, people will say that the astrologer who had read thrice this book can declare himself "Aham Eva Pandithaha". 

This book is an eye-opener. It is a corrective one. It does not accept incorrect dicta. The expression is lucid; ideas are clear; arguments are convincing; the results are correct. 

All these are due in God's Grace whom I how down again and again. (Uchchita Mahu Gangathi) 

The author(s) of Bharatiya Vidya Bhavan realised the truth in my technique: They were fully convinced, as many uncanny predictions given during the lecture, came correct and they were happy to bear the scientific explanation and to see that it came true. That is why, Governor of Bombay Dr. P. V. Chenan conferred the title "Jyechiah Marthand" and presented a Gold Medal in a convocation at Bombay to the author. 

Next it is my duty to thank these who were helpful to me to improve the knowledge in this science, to assist in my research and to bring out this lost-horn. 

Let me first thank Kulapati Mummiliji & or having appointed me as a Visiting Professor of Autology in India to deliver lectures at Delhi. Bombay and Madras regularly and occasionally in other londrina. Improvement of knowledge is mainly due to the most intelligent students (aged between 25 and 65) who would be requiring me to answer varieties of questions, and to clarify various doubts left unsolved, so far. 

Let me thank Sri K. Ganapathi, my oldest son, working in State Bank, Madras who had asked me in every aspect, deserves appreciation and my heartfelt thanks. So also, I thank Mr. Bala, Delhi, for his co-operation and assistance. 

Finally, I thank God so that this science may be developed further by the reader to give amazing, astonishing, but accurate prediction. 

# #

My final prayer to God is that this science may be used only to find auspicious time for celebration of marriage, admission in schools and colleges, construction of mansions, purchase of car, jewels, etc., admission of expectant mother in nursing home, opening account in a bank, etc., that all of us may be so happy and prosperous that astrology finds no necessity to offer mental solace, as I pray that everybody should be crowned with success. 

Peace, Picaric and Prosperity he to all of us. 

K.S.KRISHNAMURTI. 

# ABOUT THE AUTHOR

Mr. Krishnamurui, 

I would like to thank you. I want to thank you. I want to thank you because after ten months search in India, I had at last found a man who deals in the truth, the whole truth of the science of astrology. Right from last November, I began searching for or studying the science of astrology. I have met other experts and there are experts who have a great knowledge in Madras, Bangalore, right up to the North and across to the East and I thought I had met the best in this field of study, and now I know I hadn't. Because now that fortune has—or the planets have—introduced me to you. I know the cure or the quintessence of what was searching for in this science. Now I visited you at your home on the recommendation of some one in a bookshop after I had asked for someone genuine in this science. I came for ten minutes and stayed for three hours. Then in the evening I attended your claw (at Bhuraliya Vidya Bhavan) which showed how much impressed I was. Even now I am with you in the thirty-six hours of my stay in Delhi. 

The way you conduct your class was probably the most impressive thing to me because my experience with astrologers is that nowhere does a man want to give away too much of science. It is occult. There is this human element of secrecy that stops him from giving all With you, that does not apply. You gave, and gave as much as the student can absorb and $100\%$ more too. But the thing is, you gave, and you hold back nothing. You gave for the love of giving for the science that you love. And I thank you again because i am going to receive from you for many years I can say and you can say, the pile of your magazines I am taking with me to the hills. 

Regarding Your Technique, this is an Extraordinary thing. As I have said, I have studied under a number of astrologers, but I think the technique generally is the same. But yours is extraordinarily different. It changes the whole 

# xi

complexion and as a matter of fact, it fills in the obvious blanks that exist in the others. They are not consistent. Because we all recognise the truth in the science, we make allowances. We stretch our imagination a little to fill in the blanks. That should not be necessary in a science; because we recognise basically the science; we do that to fill in the blanks. 

Your personal reading of my horoscope shows also your great competence and the effectiveness of your technique and how correct it is. You told me much of the past that others have told me and much more than they told me and it was all correct. You told me about the present and that too is correct. What you told me about the future, on the basis of your predictions of the past and present, I can only assume that too will be correct and another most impressive thing I must record here is the dexterity with which you arrive to fix the periods and the times in your head as you read the chart. 

Within a matter of minutes, to my amazement, you are able to elucidate these things and which, what is more, prove correct. You are convincing, you are clear and it has been a pleasure for me, if I can say this, to study your (technique) at the peaceful hours I have on the hill. Thank you,

(Extract of Introduction at Iado-German Society, Jaipur.) 

# Pradical & Learned Members.

Mr. Krishnamurti has studied thoroughly both the Western and the Hindu system, and he openly points out the failures. He has found out a method which is popularly known as Krishna-narmurti Padbdhau or Advanced Stellus Astrology. From the Magazine published by him (Astrology and Athritsia) it is clear that hundreds of students in big cities throughout India are being educated by Mr. Krishnamurti and he has systematically Astrology in scientific lines. He delivers lectures. So, it has been decided to have a study circle so that students and scholars of Astrology can asacribble together and exchange their views, and also teach the new entrants to this field. The competent members will carry out the research study and students will assist them in collecting the data, ciicting corct horoscopie and furnishing full details Mr. Krishnamurti will put us on the right path by frequently visiting Jairpur. Tim is ever changing, nothing is stationary, modern outlook and living are absolutely different from the time of our Maharishi. Therefore, we have to render this science useful to the present day conditions, e.g., scholarship to go overseas, air travel, variation of professions, education in various subjects etc. With this view, we have started a branch of his Institute and the study circle, urided as Rajeshan Astrological Research Study Circle, inaugurated by Mr. Krishnamurtu. I take this opportunity to express our grateful thanks to the president and the Members of Indo-German Society for having extended the invitation to Mr. Krishnamurti to deliver the lectures here, whose real and valuable services are well recognised by all of us. When Mr. Krishnamurtu visited Jaipur previously under the lucky Presidentship of Honble Minister Mr. B. N. Joshi and Mr. Rameshwar Prasad Dhamani, opened a branch and inaugurated this study circle at the auspicious time. 

# ASTROLOGY-AN OCCULT SCIENCE

Astrology is a noble science. It is as old as the age of the Vedas. It depends on the position of the planets ascertained astronomically. It explains the celestial phenomena and the corresponding terrestrial events. The true meaning of Astrology is the "Message of the Stars". By using the salient principles of Astrology depending on the position of the planets ascertained astronomically one can forecast events for the benefit of all and as such, it is a useful science for interpreting nature. 

Auronomy m eni: bat n eal coe 

Up late life to have us full value. 

And not remeis thire as Ohten and Spocn 

- 

The whole world is run according to a well-defined plan. Nothing happens by chance. Astrology does not permit one to classify anything as an accident, as it explains the cause and effect of events. The divine plan is well arranged. It is timed with amazing precision. 

Some say that astrology is an art. Some others reject it as an idle dream or an illusion. Still, others may speak of astrology as though it were an altogether contemptible superstition. They contemplate with pity those who believe it. Some of those who have no disappointment or other difficulties in life take pride in saying that they have no faith in astrology and ridicule both the astrologer and the science. Probably they may fear that they may lose their self-importance if they were to recognize astrology. A few others say, under wrong impression or with prejudiced ideas, that astrology is not a science. These people would not have mastered the data on which correct predictions are based. This science explains clearly that such opponents of astrology will have in their horoscopes evil aspect between Mars and Uranus or between Mars and Mercury. These planets, when afflicted, do not give quick grasp of this science, good memory and reproductive ability; and they produce people who are either ignorant, arrogant, curious or are always inclined to find fault with what they are not able: 

Pretending to know everything, they display their ignorance. The antagonists often quote the opinions of such learned men, who do not want to admit that it is a useful science. Learning is mechanical acquisition of facts and gaining knowledge in any subject. But wisdom is not so. Astrology can be correctly interpreted only by a genious endowed with divine grace and none can call himself/wise, without knowing astrology. 

I submit that astrology is a science and that it can render very useful service to one and all and create faith even in the sceptic, if one studies this book. 

A knowledge about the history of astrology and the illustrative and eminent sages and savants who practiced astrology would give a better appreciation of the science itself. 

# HISTORY OF ASTROLOGY

The history of Astrology begins with Creation itself. Sage Garga says that the science was propounded by the Creator Himself and that Brabma handed it down to him at the time of creation. From Garga, other sage learned it and it was spread all over. It appears to be co-cial with that of the earth. 

In western countries there is a curtain belief that Seth (3,769 B.C.) was the world's first astrologer. This can be inferred from the astrological books written later by Arabic, Egyptian, Jewish and Persian writers Westerners believe that Seth was the first person to study the planets, their motions and their pathway. It is he who divided the Zodiac into twelve equal parts, as he found that the Sun ever follows a particular path in the Heavens, year after year; and he also noticed that this circular route of the Sun was spaced out by twelve full moons. Full Moon occurs once a month. Therefore the Sun's path is divided into 12 equal parts called "Mazzaroth" which term we designate as "Signs" Basis or so'.r manions. 

Around 2,600 years ago, the priests and the shepherds of Chaldea took this science for serious study and developed it. Their period was called the Golden Ages of Astrology, because 

they connected the movements of the planets with all kinds of events in human life. 

Dr. Thompson says that the Akkadins and the Samerians observed the heavens and heavenly bodies and tried to note their courses. The Babylonians and the Egyptians attributed some influence over the animate and the inanimate objects on the earth. Astrology was popular and it wielded great influence over the rich, the poor, the princes, the princes and the kings. Masprecht said, that, in his time, the Masterns of the world was Astrology. 

Some are of the opinion that Astrology had its origin in Chaldea from time immemorial. They suggest that the very name Chaldean means 'Astrologer'. The Pythagorean further advanced the concepts of the Chaldeans. They applied higher mathematics. Later, astrology came into the hands of the Greeks. They concentrated more on Naval Astrology, as they had a deep-rooted religion nature and an enquiring mind. They always posed the questions Who am I? Why am I born? What for do I live? Why are there so much of inequalities in life? They had the smarts only through astrology. 

Many of the records of the early astrologers of Nunevich and Babylon are found among the early tablets in the British Museum, some of their findings are dated nearly 3.000 years ago. 

The Greeks were also enthusiastic in following astrology. They erected the horoscope for the time of birth and presaged the finance, family, fate, fortune and future of the individuals. One of the Greek horoscopes written in Papyrus about 2,000 years ago is kept in the British Museum. The Chaldeans who practised this art of Astrology were held in high esteem even at the time of Alexander the Great. 

The Egyptians were equally interested in Astrology which played an important role. They were also responsible for shaping the future of the nation. As can be seen from the monuments, the inscriptions and modern investigations. This scienc 

dates back to 5,000 B.C Pharaohs gave much respect to the astrologers of whom Babilus was the leader. He was always consulted and the duty of Babilus was to find out the charts of those who might per chance gain power, become a rival and create trouble to the emperor. Whenever Babilus foreseaw any such native, he informed the king, who put such people to death. Pharaohs had faith in their autologet. Often they were consulted to interpret the dreams of the king 

In Peru, the lung honoured the astrologers for their sound knowledge of the science. It is only Gamaip otherwise known as "Al Halim" (meaning Learned), an astrologer in Peruian court who precisely predicted the time of birth of the prophets 

The Saracro spread the science in Spain in 711 A.D. and the North African, the Moon, in 1,237 carried the science to Europe. 

Dr. Hrcnur admits that in Chiuah about 2.75? B.I from the day of King Fu, they developed autonomy nulty for studying autology and emperor were chosen according to the profound knowledge possessed by them in autology. In 2.513 B.C. Cheuni was elected as the King in that manner. 

Whenever Alexander the Great went out, he took with him the astronomer Calmbeans in all his campaigns. He spread the science in the east by giving out some of the royal methods adopted there and his view to India had helped him to learn more and develop it further in his country. 

Hcary Corcelun Agrippa, born in 1486, was the astrologer to France I of France when he was 38 years old, John Dec was the favourite astrologer of Queen Elizabeth Albu Mczar of Bulab was the professor of Mundane Astrology at Baghdad. The Caliph Mammouarrahood translated many ancient astrological works into Arabic. 

Thus, every nation is to be credited with the knowledge of this Science. It is advisable to learn the experiences and findings 

of research workers who had contributed to the technique of correct prediction. 

Let me mention the names of a few foreign men who have contributed to the development of this Science. They were not only scholars in Astrology but were renowned and reputed Astronomers, Historians, Philosophers, Physicians and Poets.

Thus it can be seen that astrology was held in great esteem in all ages by the leaders in other sciences also. 

As years passed by, for various reasons this science, which is to live long, and which will surely live long, has lost some of its charms. But science remains ever a science. In every age, a particular science alone receives much attention and is developed, even though every science has its own innate value and is useful to us. No country had ever passed quiet without any advancement in any branch of science. So in every age any one science may be very popular, whereas the other sciences may be ignored, though not usually forgotten. It is not unlikely that there are people even now those names would come as a great surprise to all. There will be very earnest and loyal students of astrology who will popularize astrology.

Those who bring ridicule to this noble science should be silenced by producing able astrologers who will give correct knowledge to them. It is only with correct and clear understanding of the subject one can predict astoundingly accurate results, and establish that the noble legacy, astrology, given to us by our forefathers, is indeed a science which is as accurate as any other science. The present position of astrology, in the hands of a number of astrologers, is really deplorable. The excuse may be that there is no proper education to them and 

hence the result is unsatisfactory. Even when watches are manufactured by the same concern, no two watches agree. If they are manufactured by many, one can guess how they will be. Similarly, astrologers and a few other professionals usually offer different opinions, confusing the already depressed consultant: So I suggest that coaching up of students is absolutely necessary to have the same school of thought. To say that it is not a fit subject cannot be said as a wise statement from the astrologers point of view. 

In many other countries, astrology is included in the curriculum. It is understood that, in American University, Astrology is included. # Notes

Some people feel sorry that they consulted "Nada" written on palmyra leaves claimed to be written by the ancient "Rushis of India. It is a fact that the events in the lives of many persons born and yet to be born are found written already by Hindu genius. People who have consulted add that they are 

dumbfounded with the surprisingly accurate predictions about the past events, but feel upset when the future events fail miserably. This is a common complaint. Thousands of years ago, Rushis wrote these wonderful predictions. When they can be very correct in all the predictions from the time of birth of the native till the date of consultation, why they should fail in their future predictions cannot be explained. I also agree with those who say that this needs proper investigation because there are large numbers of genuine Nadis and it is likely that a few may be unauthentic ones. The solution can be found easily if the palm leaves are handed over to the consultants, by the owners, who hold the leaves and read out the results, as if from them I am confident that if the palm leaves are given to the quercet and if the reading of the past and present should agree correctly, the future must also be invariably correct when alone the Nadis can claim to be one of the panumc documents. Our saga who had written Nadis can never fail in their predictions and they have never failed, because of their intuitive power and scientific knowledge. 

It is likely that a few readers of the palm leaves gain enough knowledge and experience in reciting verses, composed by themselves in no sum. A few of them, when they read the past events, have to read very strictly the material as is found in the leaves, because the palm has to be corrected. Then only, the consultant will hear him further. But when the future is to be read, it is open to doubt as to whether he reads only those materials found on the leaves or he himself coins versus suing to the taste of the qucrist. 

In one case, a consultant and his friend caught hold of such a fraud. The Nadi reader, redhanded, because he had Mahabaratham on hand and read him life by having 'how' leaves on hand, looking at them and turning over pages after pages every 5 minutes. Another experience at Benares was also published in the magazine Astrology and Athnibus. It is a pity that the existence of a very few of such people bring ridicule to this amazing Nadi. 

Another investigation is also to be made to find out whether the documents are genuine and original. There is the doubt whether the authors, i.e., the sages, knew all languages including Tamil, etc., in South India, as they lived in the North having Sanskrit as the Mother Tongue and Nadis are found in all languages also whether they used paper and pen as some Nadis are found written in paper and claimed to be original. Whatever it is, there are records now, to prove that astrology was practiced by many people, thousands of years ago who could predict even the birth date of a native in 20th century, the place of his birth, names of his parents, occupations, etc., and the events in his life; marriage, profession, foreign journey, property, conveyance, etc. They had such profound knowledge. Now it has deteriorated to a very great extent, like a multimillionaire having a few hundred in the bank. It is more or less in a pitiable condition in India. 

In fact, there is probably no use science which is not properly understood, which w many preteed to know, and on which w many are prepaal w cipv an opium as in the case of astrology. 

Welterers are always research-minded. If they had any truth in any statement and if they are convinced, they study it further, and develop it. It may be that there are failures. Yet they consider how it is possible to predict correctly in some cases, and why in other cases there is failure; and to find out the truth, they make research till something satisfactory is discovered. 

# Astrology available data incomplete

Astrology today is incomplicit and needs to be vastly supplemented. No one is in possession of all the findings of our sages; nor are we blessed with such a Guru who can impart correct scientific knowledge to us. Whatever we may have today is only a part of what they have left behind. A subject taught by a Professor will be complete. We are not fortunate to have such an advantage in our lifetime. So what little 

literature we possess, we have to understand the fundamental principles and then, by regular and strenuous work, develop it. 

# Astrology—its Use and Limitations

Interpreted in all correctness, a knowledge of astrology does afford mental strength to the feble and weak-minded, solace to the depressed, peace to the anxious and worried, and steadiness to those who are wavering and vacillating in mind. It is a common experience that when troubles come, they come in battalions and the afflicted person gets solace from this knowledge that the time is not far off when he or her troubles would cease to exist. A full-fledged astrologer, capable of handling the subject with meticulous care, helps in no small measure to dispel the fears in the querist's mind and braces him up to face the future with confidence and hope. The astrologer helps one to have a glimpse of the unknown future: the knowledge of Destiny in store for one, stands one in good mood in nummoung difficulties that present themselves. This early knowledge renders it plausible for one to reconcile himself to the situation one finds him if in, and any severe disappointment is unlikely since one is bridged as to when, once can cherish hopes and the extent one can do so. When Dame Fortune smiles and the world appears to be full of love, few have any use for the science or for the saying 'Man proposes and God disposes'. With the frowning of fortune, cjoan mellow down, and becomes subdued. The knowledge gained through the Science helps one to be level-headed under any circumstances whether affluent or adverse. 

The knowledge of the future prompts one to render help to those who are in need, banish evil thoughts from the mind and make efforts to lead a simple, honest and pious life. The saying "Do your duty with sincerity and leave the result to God" holds out a more forceful appeal. As-tology proves that success or failure depends on our previous Karma; sufferings are due to sins committed previously and this thought helps us to be good to society, repeatedly saying "It is probably 

because of some sin committed by me in the previous birth I suffer now; let me but do harm in this life atleast to any body. 

# Branches of Astrology

The various branches of astrology are: 

(a) Medical autopsy or astro-pathology; 

(b) Astro-matcrlogy. 

(c) Mundane astrology or Judicial astrology: 

(d) Natal astrology: 

(e) Horary astrology: 

(1) Electoral astrology: 

(g) Kabala astrology: 

(h) Kralal aurology: 

(i) Omens. 

Let me explain what Natal astrology and Horary astrology mean? 

# Natal Autology

Natal astrology concerns largely with the life of human beings. A chart is made out for the moment of birth and for the particular place of birth (Latitude and Longitude being taken for calculation). 

From such a chat, one can read all events about the native: his character, temperament and peculiarities, longevity, condition of health, accident, proneness, finance and fortune, marriage, birth of children and also his prosperity or adversity. Moreover, the actual date of any occurrence in his life can be calculated. Thus natal astrology is very useful for one and all, whether he is born a King, a Kubera, or a beggar; for health and longevity are precious to every individual. Fortune, prosperity, and above all, peace of mind and happiness are desired by all. Hence natal astrology is the most useful branch of this science and therefore, it befoves all of us to support and encourage genuine research, by trained workers and 

scholars, to bridge the incomplete phases in this, just as in every other branch of science. 

It is a fact that $100\%$ correct predictions cannot be given with the literature available and with the knowledge that we may gain by studying them alone. It is only by plodding, persevering and patiently carrying out research that one will be able to fill up the gap. Supplemental, improve, and make it perfect. One of the sub-branches of Nasal Astrology may be discussed for the consideration of the readers. 

There is a wh-vanch called "Gochara Phalan" by the Hindu. Westerners call it "Transl." Let it be stated, with great humility, for the information of the reader, that the method of prediction adopted by research scholars is, in a way, an improvement over the application of the general principles of astrology handed down to us by our ancient sages and scholars. 

In the Western System, the astrologists take the radical position of the Sun at the time of birth and consider the relative positions of the Planets. Transiting in the Solar and giving their prepositions. In India and in the Hindu System, the position of the Moon at the time of birth of the native is taken as the starting and determining point to which the traveling position of the Planets are related, and according to their relative positions, we find the results and say whether the time is suspicious or not. Both the methods will be found to be incomplete and therefore use percentage of future's bound to be large. Thus cannot be of much advantage to those who desire to know their future. 

The Western and the Hindu systems of predictions based on the transits of planets fail in many cases whether referred cathcr to the Sun or to the Moon alone. 

For transitory results. Fortuna descrits serious attention as it indicates certain results which are not shown by the aspect formed by the transiting planet to those in the natal chart. 

When it is found that the results enjoyed by people horn within a few minutes of each other: show diametrically opposite 

results, we should try and find out the factor which is so fast moving as to cause opposite aspects and bring about such different effects. 

In those few minutes can planets move much? No! Then which will have a change in the position? Is it not magma thereby the other 11 magma and Fortune. 

All research scholars will surely declare that the fast changing ascendant the cups of other bodies and Fortune caused different aspects and produce different results. If therefore the cups and Fortune are also included in all calculations and predictions offered, there can be no great room for disappointment. 

Rader will do well at this stage to nuoc and ponder over the significant truth, placed before them in the preceding paragraph. Thus Autology, no doubt, is an accurate science can be proved by taking the following instances 

Idenical results are enjoyed by people who birth took place at the same minute, in the same Latitude and Longitude. Let me place before the reader in a tanlike and systematic form my lesson: 

The first instance relates to two men born at the same time and who both got married to two carers. Girls who were coming. They had no children but both couples were very fond of domestic pets, cats and dogs. The two males were lecturers producing identical results, with equal interest in politics, philosophy and religion. Minor events in their lives were also strikingly similar: for example, both suffered from toothache at the same time and on the same day. Yet, the two male partners were in no way related to each other and hailed from widely separated places 

Another instance is about two men horn in the same village who narrated their experiences after they had lived there for a fairly long time. Their temperaments, behaviour and character were identical. Both had pleasing manuocs, were always cheerful and never rude to anyone. Both were rohoad in health and whenever one fell ill, the other also asked from the same disease. 

Each of them lost a child in the same month, and had the same number of children. One was a journalist, while the other was a writer of fiction. Mercury, Mars and Jupiter were the signs who ruled over their professions. The culmination in this extraordinary similarity was in the death of those two natives on the same day. 

Yet another instance relates to a report, that appeared in a foreign journal in 1820. It mentioned that Samuel Hennings died at the age of 82. He was born on 4-6-1738 at a place situated in the same Latitude and Longitude, as King George III, who ascended the throne in October, 1760. Mr. Hennings was then an independent businessman. King George III got married on 8-9-1761 and on the same day Mr. Hennings took Elge for his wife. Both had the same number of children of each sex. Both were long-lived and died at the same hour on 2-9-1820. 

Instances can be multiplied for such remarkably coincidental happenings. The principle governing such events will be explained in my magazine. 

# Horary Astrology

The branch of science is mysterious, perfect, wonderful and most useful. After thoroughly understanding the principles, one can offer correct, clear and precise predictions without any confusion. This helps the astrologer to confirm what prediction be has to give by using other methods which, when explained, will convince and satisfy the consultant. 

Generally, the astrologer asks the quercist to give a number, at random, within 108. The number that is given forms the basis for the production. Some may scoff at this branch of science saying that the productions given by Horary Astrology cannot be correct as the number given is, after all, a chance. They may suggest that the person could have given any other number or thought of one number and mentioned another. Such people do not realize that the quercist cannot give any 

other number except the one which he had given occasionally, the lucky querist may mention a number, but the astrologer may mishear; Calculate on the misheard number. Here the divine force so works, that the number taken by the astrologer gives a clear and correct answer whereas the other number mentioned by the quenist cannot offer such a clear clue to the astrologer. They have no personal experience that it is the divine force which works and enables the astrologer to predict. The number that he gives depends upon his past action or Karma as well as the future results he is to enjoy just as the moment of birth is the effect of his past Karma. None can convince that one's birth at the particular moment, whether normal or cessation, is a chance. If one were to reiterate, one is ignorant of the wonderful Divine Law. Has he or she the choice of parents or the locality of birth? 

Generally, this branch of science is reported to, mostly by those who have no horoscopes or who doubt the correctness of them. This branch of science can answer all questions and clear all doubts. But on many occasions there are contradictory indications according to the birth charts when they try to predict using Traditional methods of prognostication: Krishnamurti's discovery is clear, convincing and correct 

On those occasions, they can make the best use of Horary Astrology for proper guidance and confirmation. Even when one decides to offer predation using other branches of the science. Horary Astrology has to be used as a final safe method to declare with confidence the results already obtained. 

This method is as rational and as scientific as any other branch of astrology and it is the sublime art of fore-seeing events from the position of the planets at the moment when one propounds seriously a question about any important matter. By applying it, one can predict the longevity, health, success or failure in one's enterprise, one's stay in foreign land or his return, the time of marriage, the description of partner, re-union of divorce, birth and death of children, sex of the child, results of the examination, recovery of lost articles, gain by lottery or 

mocs or speculation, success in litigation, treasure, legacy and anything and everything on the earth. 

This branch of science is not a bluff. It is not to dupe the gullible thorough. But at the same time, it is not easy for the students of astrology to make predictions infallibly unless they are thorough with the principles of astrology available now. 

Not Numerology: Some mistake that the astrologer uses Numerology and products. They are ignorant. The number indicates the ascendant for that query and he calculates the position of planets for that moment of judgment and then judges the result

# HORARY ASTROLOGY

# HINDU TRADITIONAL SYSTEM

# TRADITIONAL SYSTEM OF HINDUS

Let me first of all furnish the translation of various texts on Horary Asuology written by Hindu sages.. before I put forth my discovery. The reader should also know what the Westerners have propounded. 

# Piana Gyana

. Bhattacharya is the author of this work . He had commented on Varaha Mishra's works and the text deals with one of the Manches of Astrology called Horary Astrology. 

Text-books of our ages can give only the fundamental principles. The result entirely depends on the intellectual anticipation by proper application and interpretation by the astrologer without taking into consideration one's desire. Wishful thoughts and guess will prove to be useless. 

Press Gyaas—Translation of the Text. 

Stokes I: Bbottotpa bows to all th: seven planets, Sun, Moon, Mars, Mercury, Jupiter, Venus and Saturn: Then bc prays to Lord Ganapathi. He brings out for the benefit of the readers-- astrologers-- this science Prasna Gyana. 

Sloka 2: He boldly declares that Horary Astrology will never fail. He expects the astrologers to carefully judge the ten conditions of the planets after casting their exact position. 

The ten conditions of the planets are given in Jataka Parijatu and their results are explained in Saravali. 

(a) Theoptha: Jubilant, buoyant, effulgeal. A planet is in 'Theoptha' if it is in its cxahed or moolatrikona sign, i.e. it is very strong.

This means that a planet in cultivation or in Moolankow signs promises that Godows of Fortune favours the native, offers courage and moves with Victory over enemies (ll is not correct in all cases: many will die during the period of the cultivated planet).

Planets in their own sign indicate pleasure, happiness, wealth like gold, gems etc. and one can have servants at command. 

(Planets in its own sign equally causes miscries and do harm also: it is not a guarantee that such a planet should invariably do good. It depends on the lord of the constellation and the lord of the sub.) 

(c) Pramodbits: Satisfied, contated: A planet is said to be satisfied when it occupies its friend's quarters. One can find out the friend's quarters by using the following: 

Swa, Swanthya, Dbi, Dharma, Swechcha, Ayu, Sukha, i.e., count from the Moolatrikona sign of the planet whose friendly sign is to be found. The first, second, twelfth, fiftieth, ninth, eleventh sign eighah and fourth counted from the Moolatrikona signs are the friendly sign. The other signs are said to be chemical, i.e., 3, 6, 10, 11 and 7. One can easily remember that the seventh and the upachaya Sthanas counted from Moolatrikona signs are not friendly ones. The lords of the friendly signs are called the friends of the planet; the lords of the signs 3, 6, 10, 11 and 7 are said to be the enemy of that planet. It may happen that one of the two signs owned by a planet is friendly and the other is chemical. 

The authors say that such a planet owing both the friendly and enmical signs should be considered as neutral, e.g. take Sun its Moolatrihona sign is Leo Therefore Mercury owning Gemini and Virgo become the lord of the 11th and the second sign counted from Sun's Moolatrihona sign. 11th is chemical, And is friendly. So Mercury is neutral to Sun; 3rd sign Libra is owned by Venus which also rules Taurus the 10th sign from Leo, the Moolatrihona of sign of Sun, Leo. As the 3 and 10 are chemicals Venus is the enemy of Sun. Take the 4th sign Scorpio. It is owned by Mars who also governs Aris, the 9th sign. Therefore Mars is friendly with Sun. Thus one is to find out the friendship, enmity and neutral condition of the planets. 

Such a planet causes quaretment; it offers peace. It is also said that one may have damsels, riches like gems and precious metals, enjoy one's life and come out successful in one's enterprise and victorious in the disputes. (Just like friends turn out to be rogues causing danger to the person, so also planets in friend's quarters offer undesirable results to many.) 

(d) Santha: Calm, tranquil; If a planet is in the Varga of a benefic, it is said to be 'Santha'; by Bochecics, one is to mean 

benefices by nature, i.e. Juprict, Venus, Waxing Moon, and un-affected Mercury. Such a planet in Sanatha condition shows that the person will be helpful. He or she will do meritorious deeds. They will be educated and learned. They can become advisers and ministers. Hence they can enjoy life with enough financial position and have peace. 

(c) Saltha Capable, competent, efficient. A planet is in 'Saltha' condition, if it is not Moodya, Mooda and eclipsed but is with bright rays. Such a planet will bring one name, fame, reputation, honour etc. He will be liked by all. He or she has enough friends of the opposite sex: so he or she puts on good clothes, uses flower and fragrant scent (not a guarantee). 

(1) Prapeditha: Troubled tornmed. A planet is and to be in Prapcedutha, if it is defeaced by another planet in the fight among themselves. Such a planet causes separation from close relatives and friends; he or she may wander from one place to the other (frequenl transfer, keeping the family in any one place); suffer in the land of the caemcs or from ill-health. Thus he or she will be macrable, even a king will suffer (not always). 

(g) "Dheena" Unhappy, timid worried, miserable. A planet is said to be in Dheena conditions if either in Rasi Kundali or in Navamai Kundali, it occupies its enemy's quarter: such a planet threatens loss of one's position, prestige and honour. The person is defeated. He is ruined. He goes to foreign places: cannot keep himself clean (not in all cases). 

(b) "Kala -- cruci--wicked-A planet is in 'kala' condition when it occupies either in Rasi kundali or Navamai kundali, the sign belonging to any of the natural males, Sun, waning Moon, Mars, afflicted Mercury or Saturn. Such a planet always contributes for one's miserable life. 

(i) "Vikala"-unsteady, infirm, such a condition arises when a planet is eclipsed. (Saturn and Venus do not lose strength even when eclipsed. Uthrakalamintha, kenda IV 

sloka—15), loss of wealth, separation from partner, mentally worried, enemy's strength much greater and enemy becoming more powerful, agony, etc., are threadend 

(j) “Bbeedhi”, fear, threatening, frightened. A planet attains the condition of “Bbeedhi” in its Neecha, debilitated i.e., depression sign. Such a planet makes one different. There is no self-confidence. He is afraid by anything and everything. Loss of all kinds are portended. 

(Neecha Baaga Roja Yoga: Venus, friend of Mercury, neecha in Mercury's sign Venus, enemy of Jupiter is cxalted in Jupiter sign: Monn, enemy of Venus cxalted in Venus sign. 

Sloba 3: The astrologer should start his work only after bowing to the planets. He must worship, when truth will dawn in his mind. Then commence to judge the query. 

The querri has to wt facing east or north or nortb-east. He should avoid taking such a seal, facing west, south-west, north-west, south, and south-east directions. 

Varahanihira in Brihat Samhita has advised the astrologer to take seal in an even ground under a tree with flowers or fruits; he has to avoid such trees where owls and such bad omen birds take red; the name of the tree itself should be encouraging offering mental solace. Or rac should prefer Deva, Rishi Twiya, Siddha or Sddbu Nilayam with Sath pushyam, i.e., the temple, the Ashram of Maharishis, the residences of Brahmins, the places of Siddha Purushas or good Sadbus where there are planets with beautiful and sweet smelling flowers etc. Why? The sight itself should be pleasing to the eyes. Lawn is preferred. 

Sleks 4: The consultant also should pray with fruits, flowers, gems and gold; then only, come out with his problems and put queries to the astrologer. 

Avoid taking seat under a tree which is cut or which is thorny. Avoid gravyards, neglected temples, junction of the roads, dirty places, and dry barren ground. Reject such places 

where persons remain naked, or saloon, slaughter house gambling den, hospitals, prison or honey store room. 

Why because one can have favourable results if the consultant faces east. If he faces south or north, journey is indicated. South-west and north-east show that there is long delay in achieving one's aim. North-west and south-east threaten failure, disappointment or temporary pleasure. 

Regarding west, in Prana Bairava it is taken as auspicious whereas Varahamihira advices to avoid west. 

Both the astrologer and the consultant must prefer the morning hours to the afternoon the Santhyakala, twilight period and the night. 

Necelakanta suggests that the astrologer should check whether the consultant has approached him with the sincere idea of placing his problems and then requesting the astrologer to solve them or be has come to test him or put some questions casually. This can be judged by finding out whether the lagna that is rising in the cau is occupied by Moon, squared or oppo- sed by Saturn, or opposed by Mercury or aspected by Mars and Mercury in mowdyam, i.c. eclipsed If the ascendant, at the moment of query, has such afflictions, the consultant is not sincere. Benefits in the Lagna Bhava denotes that bc is truc and he has the real urge. Malefics in the lagna indicates that he is not plain and open If lord of the 7th cusp receives aspects from its enemy or Jurvier or Mercury be is crooked and not straightforward But if the 7th house as well as lagna receive aspects from either Moon or Mercury or Jupiter or by all of them he is honest when he puts the query Benefits aspecting the enemy of lord of 7 when he aspects the latter, then also, he is honest. 

Only when the consultant is serious and sincere, then only truth will come out; prediction will prove to be correct. 

After satisfying himself, the astrologer has to note down the various questions, 1, 2, 3, and so on, if the person wants to consult more than one question. While judging the first 

question, take magma as the first Bhava, for the second question and where Moon is deposited. Consider that sign as Laguna; for the third question, note the sign teamed by Sun and take that sign as Laguna. For the fourth, the magma should be the sign occupied by Jupiter; the fifth question is to be answered by taking either of the signs occupied by the stronger or the two planets Mercury or Venus and so on

It is advisable to read Brhat Samhita where Varahamihira has elaborately dealt with 'omeros'.

Sbola 15. If the fixed sign Taurus, Leo, Scorpio or Aquarius be the ascendant, one cannot be defeated; there will be no loss; disease will continue and cannot be cured; journey will not be made: but one can have the rank or position which she expect 

Slate 16 If any of the movable signs Arin, Cancer, Libra or Capricorn be the ascendant, one will be defeated, things will be lost, disease will disappear, journey will be made but one cannot have the rank or position or improvement in status.

One is to consider the first half as though it is a fixed sign and offer much prediction as in given for a fixed sign: the second half is to be considered as a movable sign and predictivcus given for a movable sign is to be applied for the second half of the dual or common or Ubaya sign.
